 stands for Individual Academic Plan. Your <a href="http://www.cpp.edu/advising/iap" target="_blank">
IAP</a> is a snapshot of your <a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">
MyPlanner</a> filled out to your anticipated graduation date.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p style="line-height:15.0pt"><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#2A2A2A">In April, 5,750 students who were within 0-60 of graduating received the notice to complete their
<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/advising/iap" target="_blank">IAP</a> on their BroncoDirect To Do list.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p style="line-height:15.0pt"><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#2A2A2A">For more information on the
<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/advising/iap" target="_blank">IAP</a> and <a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">
MyPlanner</a>, as well as contact information for advisors, visit <a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">
www.cpp.edu/advising/myplanner/index.shtml</a><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">.</span></strong><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<td style="background:#231F20;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><img border="0" width="680" height="40" id="_x0000_i1034" src="http://www.cpp.edu/semester/newsletter/img/5tips-spring2017.png" alt="5 TIPS FOR PLANNING FOR SEMESTER CONVERSION"></span><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr style="height:164.25pt">
<td valign="top" style="padding:7.5pt 6.0pt 7.5pt 7.5pt;height:164.25pt">
<ol start="1" type="1">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#2A2A2A;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:15.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Find out if you can graduate under the quarter system by filling our
<a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">MyPlanner</a>.<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#2A2A2A;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:15.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Complete any sequence courses you have already started under quarters. This will make the transition more straight forward.<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#2A2A2A;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:15.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">If you need a class not being offered in the quarter that you need it, be sure to tell your department. Many departments are keeping track of student demand and adding sections when demand is high.<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#2A2A2A;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:15.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Annual tuition will be divided into two payments once the campus switches to semesters for 2018-19. (Under quarters, payments are divided into three payments.)<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#2A2A2A;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:15.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">For assistance with
<a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">MyPlanner</a> or filling out your
<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/advising/iap" target="_blank">IAP</a>, visit your college’s advising center or seek out your Student Success Ambassador. You can find contacts
<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~advising/for-students/index.shtml" target="_blank">here</a>.
<o:p></o:p></span></li></ol>
</td>
</tr>

<tr style="height:162.75pt">
<td valign="top" style="background:#DEEDBE;padding:7.5pt 6.0pt 7.5pt 7.5pt;height:162.75pt">
<p style="line-height:15.0pt"><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#2A2A2A">Summer session is offering
<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~summer/schedule.shtml" target="_blank">more than 650 courses</a>, including many high demand classes. You may be able to complete one or more of your degree requirements and make summer your “fast pass to graduation.” A second summer
 registration period for students will begin May 22 and end June 8. Summer Add/Drop begins June 12.
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p style="line-height:15.0pt"><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#2A2A2A"><a href="http://www.cpp.edu/summer" target="_blank"></a></span><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_3" o:spid="_x0000_s1026" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="It's not too late to register for summer classes" href="http://www.cpp.edu/summer" target="&quot;_blank&quot;" style='position:absolute;margin-left:260.05pt;margin-top:0;width:311.25pt;height:158.25pt;z-index:251659264;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square;mso-width-percent:0;mso-height-percent:0;mso-wrap-distance-left:0;mso-wrap-distance-top:0;mso-wrap-distance-right:0;mso-wrap-distance-bottom:0;mso-position-horizontal:right;mso-position-horizontal-relative:text;mso-position-vertical:absolute;mso-position-vertical-relative:line;mso-width-percent:0;mso-height-percent:0;mso-width-relative:page;mso-height-relative:page' o:allowoverlap="f" o:button="t">

<w:wrap type="square" anchory="line"/>

<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/%7Esummer/finaid.shtml" target="_blank">financial aid</a>, including some grant money, is available for Cal Poly Pomona students who have applied for financial aid and have remaining eligibility for the 2016-17 school year.
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p style="line-height:15.0pt"><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#2A2A2A">“We really want to encourage students to take advantage of the summer sessions,” says Sepehr Eskandari, interim associate vice president for academic
 planning and faculty affairs. “It’s a great way to take required courses, especially those in high demand, and stay on track for graduation.”<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<td style="background:#231F20;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><img border="0" width="680" height="40" id="_x0000_i1032" src="http://www.cpp.edu/semester/newsletter/img/data-spring2017.png" alt="MyPLANNER DATA BEING USED TO SCHEDULE SUMMER, FALL &amp; WINTER CLASSES"></span><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr style="height:89.25pt">
<td valign="top" style="padding:7.5pt 6.0pt 7.5pt 7.5pt;height:89.25pt">
<p style="line-height:15.0pt"><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#2A2A2A">Colleges and departments are using
<a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">MyPlanner</a> aggregated data to plan their courses through spring quarter 2018. Where demand is high for seats, colleges are trying to add course sections when they can. As more
 students complete <a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">
MyPlanner</a>, the data will provide departments with increasingly accurate forecasts of course demand. If there are impacted classes that you need, be sure to complete your
<a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~advising/myplanner/index.shtml" target="_blank">MyPlanner</a>.
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</td>
</tr>

<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK198"></a><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Hey Bronco,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><br>
We wanted to give you six tips to help you get ready for winter 2018 registration and semester conversion. Here are the first two:&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">1. Check your Degree Progress Report to see your remaining degree requirements, especially if you're close to graduation.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">
 You can find this tool in your BroncoDirect Student Center.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">2. Turn in any academic petitions and paperwork, such as Grade Forgiveness.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">
 If you have any paperwork to do, don't wait until the last minute.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">General registration for winter 2018 begins October 30.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">We also wanted to share a quick chart that shows you the differences between quarters and semesters.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">What's changing in Fall 2018, and what's staying the same?&nbsp;</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

</td>

<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Quarters</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</td>
<td width="195" valign="top" style="width:136.25pt;border-top:solid black 1.0pt;border-left:none;border-bottom:none;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;background:#CBCBCB;padding:2.25pt 2.25pt 2.25pt 2.25pt;height:21.0pt">
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Semesters</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

</td>
<td width="195" valign="top" style="width:136.25pt;border:none;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;padding:2.25pt 2.25pt 2.25pt 2.25pt;height:21.0pt">

<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 5.25pt 6.0pt">
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK198"></a><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Hey Bronco,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><br>
We wanted to give you six tips to help you get ready for winter 2018 registration and semester conversion.&nbsp;<a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ukui8r8ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2F7qRsXx" target="_blank">We gave you two last week</a>.
 Here are the next two:&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">3. Attend a one-on-one or group advising session with your academic advisor.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">
 To find your faculty or staff advisor, visit <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ukui8r8ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2FV84CFz" target="_blank">
Student Success Central's advising directory</a>.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">4. Plan for at least 15 units.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">&nbsp;Taking at least 15 units every
 quarter puts you on track to graduate in four years (if you're a freshman) or two years (if you're a transfer student).&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">General registration for winter 2018 begins October 30.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">We also wanted to share a quick chart that shows you the differences between quarters and semesters.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">What's changing in Fall 2018, and what's staying the same?&nbsp;</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal">Subject<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">SEMESTER CONVERSION:&nbsp; ECE 109/L<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Dear Students,<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">After semester conversion the lecture and laboratory course sequences 109-207-209 will be offered as a two course sequence:&nbsp; 1101-2101 with corresponding labs.&nbsp; ECE 1101 will cover material from 109 and the first half of 207 and ECE 2101
 will cover material from the second half of 207 and 209.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">To help with semester conversion, beginning next quarter (Winter 2018) ECE 109 and ECE 109L will no longer be offered.&nbsp; Instead you should take ECE 299 (<span style="color:black">Topic: ECE 1101 in Semester) and ECE 299L (Topic: ECE 1101L
 in Semester).&nbsp; These courses will give you credit for semester courses:&nbsp; ECE 1101 and ECE 1101L (109/L and half of 207/L) and serve as prerequisites for semester courses ECE 2101 and ECE 2101L (the second half of 207/L and 209/L)<b><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Verdana&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Best Regards,<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">The ECE Department<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class="MsoNormal">Dear students,<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Next quarter, instead of enrolling in ECE 220L you should instead enroll in ECE 299L section numbers (11 through 19).&nbsp; Note a subset of these sections will be offered.&nbsp; This course will give you credit for the semester course ECE 2200L.&nbsp;
 For EE majors ECE 2200L is equivalent to ECE 220L.&nbsp; For CpE majors ECE 2200L is equivalent to both ECE 325L and ECE 220L.&nbsp; If you are a CpE major, and you take ECE 299L and you previously took ECE 299 (equivalent to 220) you will receive credit for ECE 325
 and ECE 325L.&nbsp; If you are a CpE and you took ECE 220, then you are, again, strongly advised to take ECE 325/L before semester conversion; you would then not want to take ECE 299L.<o:p></o:p></p>

<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Winter 2018 Advising and Semester Conversion Guide:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">This year, the ECE department is conducting winter 2018 advising online. The theme is semester conversion and things you should know before Fall 2018. All the documents and other important information can be found here:&nbsp;<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~asalaheddin/semester_conversion/">http://www.cpp.edu/~asalaheddin/semester_conversion/</a>.
 The page will be updated regularly to reflect the most up to date information and new semester-related forms.<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Freshman advising:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">If you are a first year student, you can read the conversion guide; however, you need not fill the online form. You are still required to check with the advising center for your mandatory advising session.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Advising Hold:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">To lift your advising hold, you should go to the&nbsp;<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~asalaheddin/semester_conversion/">Semester Conversion Guide page</a>&nbsp;and watch your major’s video. &nbsp; &nbsp;The documents shown in the video can also be found on the
 same page. Once you have watched the video and reviewed the other documents, head to the link in the video to the sign-in the online form. If you have priority registration, you must fill the form by
<b>1/23/2018</b> and you must indicate that you have priority registration on the form. If you have regular registration, you must fill the form by
<b>1/26/2018</b> to get your hold removed on time. &nbsp;The whole process shouldn’t take you more than 30 minutes to complete.<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Semester Conversion online forum:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">The ECE department has launched an online forum to collect and answer all semester conversion related questions. The best and quickest way to find answers is to post your question there, you can also answer some of the questions yourself.
 To sign-up and post questions in the form, go to:&nbsp;<span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:#30424D;background:white"><a href="http://piazza.com/csupomona/winter2018/ece000">piazza.com/csupomona/winter2018/ece000</a>&nbsp;and register
 using your cpp email. If you are having problems signing in to forum, tell us here:&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:#444444"><a href="https://goo.gl/jSwsvz">https://goo.gl/jSwsvz</a></span><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:#1F497D"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Hello,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">For those of you who missed the email below it was sent out on Friday, January 19, 2018&nbsp; at 4:52 PM.&nbsp; This&nbsp; email provides the information and instructions for Winter 18
 Advising and for you to get your hold removed.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Removing the HOLDS&nbsp; -&nbsp; If you have watched the video and completed all the instructions for the ECE advising your name will be generated on a list that will be provided to
 me to REMOVE THE HOLD.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Please Note:&nbsp; The goal is to remove the Priority Holds before January 31, 2018, for Priority Registration.&nbsp; All other holds will be removed before February 5, 2018 the first
 day Spring 18 Registration.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">I will ONLY REMOVE HOLDS from the List Generated from you watching the video online.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">You do not need to check with me about your hold being removed unless it is the day before you are going to register.

<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Winter 2018 Advising and Semester Conversion Guide:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">This year, the ECE department is conducting winter 2018 advising online. The theme is semester conversion and things you should know before Fall 2018. All the documents and other important information can be found here:&nbsp;<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~asalaheddin/semester_conversion/">http://www.cpp.edu/~asalaheddin/semester_conversion/</a>.
 The page will be updated regularly to reflect the most up to date information and new semester-related forms.<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Freshman advising:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">If you are a first year student, you can read the conversion guide; however, you need not fill the online form. You are still required to check with the advising center for your mandatory advising session.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Advising Hold:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">To lift your advising hold, you should go to the&nbsp;<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~asalaheddin/semester_conversion/">Semester Conversion Guide page</a>&nbsp;and watch your major’s video. &nbsp; &nbsp;The documents shown in the video can also be found on the
 same page. Once you have watched the video and reviewed the other documents, head to the link in the video to the sign-in the online form. If you have priority registration, you must fill the form by
<b>1/23/2018</b> and you must indicate that you have priority registration on the form. If you have regular registration, you must fill the form by
<b>1/26/2018</b> to get your hold removed on time. &nbsp;The whole process shouldn’t take you more than 30 minutes to complete.<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Semester Conversion online forum:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">The ECE department has launched an online forum to collect and answer all semester conversion related questions. The best and quickest way to find answers is to post your question there, you can also answer some of the questions yourself.
 To sign-up and post questions in the form, go to:&nbsp;<span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:#30424D;background:white"><a href="http://piazza.com/csupomona/winter2018/ece000">piazza.com/csupomona/winter2018/ece000</a>&nbsp;and register
 using your cpp email. If you are having problems signing in to forum, tell us here:&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:#444444"><a href="https://goo.gl/jSwsvz">https://goo.gl/jSwsvz</a></span><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:12.0pt"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>

<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 5.25pt 6.0pt">
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK198"></a><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Hey Bronco,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><br>
We've given you five tips so far (<a href="http://campaign.r20.constantcontact.com/render?ca=7cfecb73-0466-4233-903e-b9dd91bd6f64&amp;preview=true&amp;m=1119858940488&amp;id=preview" target="_blank">here</a> and
<a href="http://campaign.r20.constantcontact.com/render?ca=1ab15950-5b89-44b1-9bb9-887253ae59ef&amp;preview=true&amp;m=1119858940488&amp;id=preview" target="_blank">
here</a>) about getting ready for spring 2018 registration&nbsp;and semester conversion.&nbsp;Here are the last two:&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">6. Plan to continue or finish any sequences you've started.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">&nbsp;If
 you don't finish a sequence before semesters, the academic department will offer options to complete it. But for now, if you can, plan on finishing the sequences you've started before conversion.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">7. Finish any lower-division General Education areas you've started, especially Area D.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">&nbsp;We
 received a lot of questions about this tip last quarter. Lower-division&nbsp;General Education requirements are changing slightly in semesters, especially Area D. Taking care of these courses now will help you have a smoother transition, but don't worry if you
 can't finish them --&nbsp;you'll work with your academic advisor to come up with a plan.&nbsp;Waiting to take upper-division synthesis courses until semesters is okay.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">And if you haven't already, take a look at&nbsp;the&nbsp;<a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=6hsijc7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2FSQTH7F" target="_blank">Semester
 Conversion website</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- it has the Conversion Guide, a student handbook and tons of other resources.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">General registration for spring 2018 runs from February 5-23. Your enrollment appointment is posted in your Student Center.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Dear Students,<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">There are problems with prerequisite checking in Bronco Direct.&nbsp; If you are having problems adding courses, try the following<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="text-indent:-.25in">1)<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:105%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>Make sure that you have not exceeded&nbsp; the number of units that you are allowed (for example 16 during pre-registration)<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="text-indent:-.25in">2)<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:105%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>Empty your shopping cart, and try again<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="text-indent:-.25in">3)<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:105%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>Empty your shopping cart, logout, and try again<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="text-indent:-.25in">4)<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:105%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>If you took ECE 299/L, it may be that the system is not recognizing this as the prerequisite for a follow on course.&nbsp; If you try to register and this is the case,<span style="color:#1F497D">
</span>take a screen shot of the error message. Provide a copy of the error message and your transcript to<span style="color:#1F497D">
</span>the instructor of record that is teaching the <b><span style="color:red">section</span> of course</b> that you would like to add and they can issue you<span style="color:#1F497D">
</span>a permission number.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:10.0pt">We are sorry for any inconvenience<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:10.0pt">The ECE Deaprtment</span><o:p></o:p></p>

<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">If you're transitioning to semesters, you should be playing
<a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=9qkfkf7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Esemester%2Fthe-game.shtml" target="_blank">
Semester Conversion: The Game</a>. Completing levels enters you to win opportunity drawings for spring 2018 parking permits, CPP swag, theme park tickets, Bronco Bucks and tons more.&nbsp;The rules are super easy:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
</div>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">1. Pick up a game card from the Bronco Advising Center or your college's advising center, or download one
<a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=9qkfkf7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Esemester%2Fthe-game.shtml" target="_blank">
on the website</a>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">2. Complete the tasks within each level. It's your choice to stop at Level 1, or go all the way to Levels 2 or 3.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">3. Turn in your card to the BAC by
<strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">March 8 at 5 p.m.&nbsp;</span></strong></span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Dear Student,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Thank you for your email but due to the influx of student appointments and emails during this registration window, please allow 48 hours for an email response.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

 college/department.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<body lang="EN-US" link="blue" vlink="purple">
<div class="WordSection1">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Students,</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Spring 2018 Parking Permits are available for sale.</span></b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span></b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">You may purchase your permit at:
<a href="https://csupomona.t2hosted.com/Account/Portal">https://csupomona.t2hosted.com/Account/Portal</a> &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Your login credentials will be the same as your Cal Poly Pomona email login. Please click LOGIN at the upper right of the page to log in.
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">When ordering your permit, <b>
<u>please be sure your mailing address is correct so your permit is delivered to you</u>.</b></span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Once you place your order, you should receive your permit in 5 to 7 business days. You will receive an email confirmation of your order and from that email you can print a temporary permit that is valid for
 10 days from the date of purchase. <b>Be sure to print out the temporary permit and display it on your dash until your regular permit arrives.</b>
</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Permits are effective for use starting Friday, March 23, 2018.</span></b><span style="font-size:12.0pt"> Please hang your permit from your rear view mirror and be sure it is visible when parked on campus.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><u>Permit prices are as follows</u>:<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Quarterly permits: $154<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Daily permits: $8<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Hourly permits: $2 per hour<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">You can find information on where to park at
<a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~parking/index.shtml">http://www.cpp.edu/~parking/index.shtml</a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Feel free to contact us for any questions or concerns at
<a href="mailto:parking@cpp.edu">parking@cpp.edu</a> or 909-869-3061 and we will be glad to help you!
</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Thank you, </span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Parking and Transportation Services</span><o:p></o:p></p>

<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 0in 6.0pt">
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><b><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Semester Conversion Financial Literacy Workshop Recap<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK19"></a><span style="display:none"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div align="center">
<table class="MsoNormalTable" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="width:100.0%" id="content_LETTER.BLOCK19">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 5.25pt 6.0pt">
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">In February, we co-hosted a workshop with the Office of Financial Aid &amp; Scholarships, Student Accounting &amp; Cashiering Services, and the Cal Poly Federal Credit
 Union about the changes to student accounting and financial aid. If you weren't able to attend, here's a recap:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
</div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><u><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Student Accounting</span></u></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">Semester Conversion will not affect overall tuition costs.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">In semesters, you'll pay twice per year instead of three times per year. The price per term will be higher than you're used to because it's being split into two payments instead of three.<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">Continue to monitor your CPP email for reminder messages from Student Accounting &amp; Cashiering Services.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><u><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Financial Aid</span></u></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">Semester Conversion will not affect the amount of financial aid you may receive. The Office of Financial Aid &amp; Scholarships will continue to award you based on the information you submit on your
 FAFSA.<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">In semesters, you'll receive your aid twice per year instead of three times per year. If you receive a refund, you'll need to budget accordingly.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">Continue to monitor your CPP email for messages from Financial Aid &amp; Scholarships, complete your BroncoDirect Student Center To Do List items and report any changes in your family's financial
 situation.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><u><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Budgeting</span></u></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">The Cal Poly Federal Credit Union has tons of
<a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.calpolyfcu.org%2Fstart-your-student-budget-today%2F" target="_blank">
resources</a> and <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.calpolyfcu.org%2Fbanner%2Fits-a-money-thing%2F" target="_blank">
videos</a> about how to create a student budget.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<div>
<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">And one last FYI:
<strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">fall 2018 fees will be due July 26</span></strong>.
<strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">The deadline for financial aid students to pay any outstanding balance for fall 2018 will be in September.&nbsp;</span></strong><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>

<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><img border="0" width="5" height="1" id="_x0000_i1029" src="http://img.constantcontact.com/letters/images/sys/S.gif"><o:p></o:p></p>

<div align="center">
<table class="MsoNormalTable" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="width:100.0%" id="content_LETTER.BLOCK9">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 0in 6.0pt">
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Demystifying Semester Conversion</span></strong><b><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK10"></a><span style="display:none"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div align="center">
<table class="MsoNormalTable" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="width:100.0%" id="content_LETTER.BLOCK10">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 5.25pt 6.0pt">
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">We know that a lot of information about Semester Conversion can be confusing, but we want to make it as easy as possible to understand. Here are a few answers
 to some questions we've been getting:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">You will not lose credit for courses you've already taken in the quarter system.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Esemester%2Ffor-students%2Fstudent-pledge.shtml" target="_blank">The
 Semester Conversion pledge</a> states that there should be no loss of credits applied to your degree requirements earned before Semester Conversion.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Every student who's transitioning to semesters has the options of staying on their quarter curriculum or switching
 to a semester curriculum.&nbsp;</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Watch this video to understand what those options mean:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D0pksBR1cGU0" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:none"><img border="0" width="382" height="212" id="_x0000_i1030" src="https://mlsvc01-prod.s3.amazonaws.com/84a5bccb401/53b433fa-d7a9-401d-bcda-6810f90ca598.png" hspace="5" vspace="5" alt="An illustration of one horse asking another how to plan for semesters." name="ACCOUNT.IMAGE.209"></span></a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D0pksBR1cGU0" target="_blank">Understanding
 Your Curriculum Year</a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">There's a mathematical difference between quarter and semester units.&nbsp;</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">You might notice in the Conversion Guide that a class you need to take is turning from a 4-unit course into a 3-unit course. This is because of the term length.
 If you stay on a quarter curriculum, the 3-unit semester courses you take become 4.5 quarter units to go toward your overall 180&#43; unit degree requirement.&nbsp;Watch this video to understand the conversion, and what happens if you switch to a quarter curriculum:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DOC4PU6sHb9w" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:none"><img border="0" width="382" height="212" id="_x0000_i1031" src="https://mlsvc01-prod.s3.amazonaws.com/84a5bccb401/8bc62244-93a9-42f5-9630-1134996db749.png" hspace="5" vspace="5" alt="An illustration of one horse asking another how units convert." name="ACCOUNT.IMAGE.210"></span></a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DOC4PU6sHb9w" target="_blank">Understanding
 Unit Conversion</a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Grade forgiveness, course repetition, course withdrawal and other academic policies will still be in place.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">The university is still working on rewriting these policies for semesters. We'll communicate with you when the new policies are available.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><img border="0" width="5" height="1" id="_x0000_i1032" src="http://img.constantcontact.com/letters/images/sys/S.gif"><o:p></o:p></p>

<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 0in 6.0pt">
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Semester Conversion Toolbox</span></strong><b><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
</td>
</tr>

<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK40"></a><span style="display:none"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div align="center">
<table class="MsoNormalTable" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="width:100.0%" id="content_LETTER.BLOCK40">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 5.25pt 6.0pt">
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Do you know what's in your Semester Conversion toolbox? Here are your tools:&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo4">
<strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">Your <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fdirectories%2Fadvising-directory.shtml" target="_blank">
academic advisor</a>,</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif"> who can help you navigate your curriculum choice.</span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo4">
<strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">Your <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DF70rzOaM3yI" target="_blank">
Degree Progress Report</a> and your <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Eadvising%2Fmyplanner%2Findex.shtml" target="_blank">
MyPlanner</a>,</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif"> which can help you do your longterm academic planning.</span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo4">
<strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">The <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Esemester%2Fconversion-guide.shtml" target="_blank">
Conversion Guide</a>,</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif"> which tells you how quarter courses translate into semester courses.</span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo4">
<strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">The <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Esemester%2Ffor-students%2Fhandbook.shtml" target="_blank">
Semester Conversion Student Handbook</a>,</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif"> which outlines a lot of information about the changes (like unit conversion, changes to GE, course scheduling and more).</span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo4">
<strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">The <a href="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=bhmuus7ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Esemester%2Findex.shtml" target="_blank">

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#1F497D">FYI<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#1F497D"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div>
<div style="border:none;border-top:solid #E1E1E1 1.0pt;padding:3.0pt 0in 0in 0in">
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">From:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"> H. Erkan Ozkaya

<b>Subject:</b> Electrical/Computer Engineering Students for NASA-CPP Business Startup Program<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Subject Line:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;E</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">lectrical/Computer Engineering
 Students for NASA-CPP Business Startup Program</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">We are looking for a three&nbsp;Electrical/Computer Engineering or Engineering Technology&nbsp;students with a passion for electronics&nbsp;for the NASA-CPP Business Startup Program. &nbsp;Positions are related
 to to rapid prototyping circuits for projects utilizing optical fibers.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">The NASA-CPP Business Startup Program is a Cal Poly Pomona sponsored organization that commercializes NASA technology as well as our own innovative ideas. The program has won several grants
 and awards, including the Outstanding Partnership Award,&nbsp;Federal Laboratory Consortium&nbsp;Far West Regional, Bronco Startup Challenge, and President’s Discovery Fellowship Award. We are starting right away this semester, so applicants are asked to apply immediately
 to be involved as soon as possible.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Benefits of getting involved in this program:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Resume booster: Several of our previous team members got full time jobs and/or internships at NASA, JPL, Northrop Grumman, U.S. Air Force, Aerospace Corp., Walt
 Disney Corporation, Universal Studios, PepsiCo, DHL, Southern California Edison, Kaiser Permanente, Johnson and Johnson, Citi National Bank, Enterprise, and Extron Electronics.</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Course credit: You can receive 4 units of business course credit per semester.&nbsp;<br>
• A &quot;Learn by Doing&quot; approach to developing your technical skills</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Unique Experience: You will gain unique experience in engineering analysis often used in industry, marketing, and entrepreneurship, product pitching (in competitions
 similar to Shark Tank) by working with cross-functional teams (business, engineering, art etc.)&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Responsibilities and Duties:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">The student engineers will be responsible for:</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Circuit design and implementation as printed circuit boards (PCBs)</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Attending the weekly NASA-CPP meetings (Fridays at 2:30PM) to report on weekly progress</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Develop, and construct prototypes as needed for related projects&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Sourcing of manufacturing</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Collaborating with physics, business, and other engineering students</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Design test and procedures for testing</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Preparing reports/documentation/presentations to communicate technical results</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Required Qualifications:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">In order to obtain this position, the engineering student must be:</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Experience with electronics prototyping</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Self-motivated&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">•&nbsp;Able to work with limited supervision</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Deliver progress weekly while taking courses at CPP</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Studying a related engineering major or have applicable experience&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Excellent at written and verbal communication</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• A team player&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Graduating Spring 2020 or later</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<div class="WordSection1">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#1F497D">Dear
</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Electrical/Computer Engineering and Engineering Technology&nbsp;students,</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#1F497D"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#1F497D"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:#1F497D"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">We are looking for a three&nbsp;Electrical/Computer Engineering or Engineering Technology&nbsp;students with a passion for electronics&nbsp;for the NASA-CPP Business Startup Program. &nbsp;Positions are related
 to to rapid prototyping circuits for projects utilizing optical fibers.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">The NASA-CPP Business Startup Program is a Cal Poly Pomona sponsored organization that commercializes NASA technology as well as our own innovative ideas. The program has won several grants
 and awards, including the Outstanding Partnership Award,&nbsp;Federal Laboratory Consortium&nbsp;Far West Regional, Bronco Startup Challenge, and President’s Discovery Fellowship Award. We are starting right away this semester, so applicants are asked to apply immediately
 to be involved as soon as possible.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Benefits of getting involved in this program:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Resume booster: Several of our previous team members got full time jobs and/or internships at NASA, JPL, Northrop Grumman, U.S. Air Force, Aerospace Corp., Walt
 Disney Corporation, Universal Studios, PepsiCo, DHL, Southern California Edison, Kaiser Permanente, Johnson and Johnson, Citi National Bank, Enterprise, and Extron Electronics.</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Course credit: You can receive 4 units of business course credit per semester.&nbsp;<br>
• A &quot;Learn by Doing&quot; approach to developing your technical skills</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Unique Experience: You will gain unique experience in engineering analysis often used in industry, marketing, and entrepreneurship, product pitching (in competitions
 similar to Shark Tank) by working with cross-functional teams (business, engineering, art etc.)&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Responsibilities and Duties:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">The student engineers will be responsible for:</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Circuit design and implementation as printed circuit boards (PCBs)</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Attending the weekly NASA-CPP meetings (Fridays at 2:30PM) to report on weekly progress</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Develop, and construct prototypes as needed for related projects&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Sourcing of manufacturing</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Collaborating with physics, business, and other engineering students</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Design test and procedures for testing</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Preparing reports/documentation/presentations to communicate technical results</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Required Qualifications:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">In order to obtain this position, the engineering student must be:</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Experience with electronics prototyping</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Self-motivated&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">•&nbsp;Able to work with limited supervision</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Deliver progress weekly while taking courses at CPP</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Studying a related engineering major or have applicable experience&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Excellent at written and verbal communication</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• A team player&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Graduating Spring 2020 or later</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Preferred Skills:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">It would be preferred for the engineering student to have experience with:</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• PCB design software</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• 3D modeling software</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
