<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Subject Line: ME students for NASA-CPP Business Startup Program</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">We have two positions open for students at NASA-CPP Business Startup Program (<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fnasacpp.org%2F&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7Cf92bdae0a3a74e83ad9108d61020ee1a%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636714131106692626&amp;sdata=Rhu8qWmJRyUvv3lFVhR6nvT6Gk%2FaGJDAd1LdGVccHic%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://nasacpp.org/" shash="ttKDBcsR4woE&#43;5om72IW8ORAidZhyLNmKm4fyNpByQnFykxxopuKMlTVtgWnTZ7JnulHm3VoNypXH71bR9YiE0X4he5Xn7jsAcqdomB6bUIA2Uxs/h3sorGBFqYJpZWi6fxUKHnr9NiQbN4Jj&#43;wTwbXw7UBoyxnFKAI1M5sTXbA=">nasacpp.org</a>).&nbsp;<span style="font-size:9.0pt">The
 student engineer will participate in the NASA CPP Business Startup BSP program on the Mobile Microscope project. NASA-CPP BSP&nbsp;projects and its partnership with NASA has won several awards including the Outstanding Partnership Award,&nbsp;Federal Laboratory Consortium&nbsp;Far
 West Regional 2017. Former students who participated in this program got internships and jobs in top organizations including NASA and JPL. The mobile microscope is a portable and affordable microscope designed to work in conjunction with a smartphone and provide
 magnification levels high enough to view blood cells.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Benefits of getting involved in this program:</span></b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Resume booster: Several of our previous team members got full time jobs and/or&nbsp;internships at NASA, JPL, etc.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Course credit: You can receive 4 units of course credit per quarter. In some cases, this may count as a graduation project.&nbsp; (This is not a paid position)<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Unique Experience: You will gain unique experience in product design, marketing, and entrepreneurship, product pitching (in competitions similar to Shark Tank) by working with cross-functional
 teams (business, engineering, art, etc.)&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Responsibilities and Duties</span></b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">The student engineer will be responsible for:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Attending the weekly NASA-CPP meetings (Fridays 2:30pm-5:30pm) to report on weekly progress<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Coming up with creative design solutions to improve product’s function<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Prototyping of the hardware<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Sourcing of manufacturing<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Collaborating with physics, business, and other engineering students<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Designing test and procedures for testing<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Preparing reports/documentation/presentations to communicate technical results&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Required Qualifications</span></b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">In order to obtain this position, the engineering student must be:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3">

<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Able to 3D print<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Studying a related engineering major<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Excellent at written and verbal communication<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">A team player&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">Preferred Skills</span></b><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif">It would be preferred for the engineering student to have experience with:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal">We have two positions open for the Aerospace and ME students at NASA-CPP Business Startup Program (<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fnasacpp.org%2F&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7Cf92bdae0a3a74e83ad9108d61020ee1a%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636714131106692626&amp;sdata=Rhu8qWmJRyUvv3lFVhR6nvT6Gk%2FaGJDAd1LdGVccHic%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://nasacpp.org/" shash="ttKDBcsR4woE&#43;5om72IW8ORAidZhyLNmKm4fyNpByQnFykxxopuKMlTVtgWnTZ7JnulHm3VoNypXH71bR9YiE0X4he5Xn7jsAcqdomB6bUIA2Uxs/h3sorGBFqYJpZWi6fxUKHnr9NiQbN4Jj&#43;wTwbXw7UBoyxnFKAI1M5sTXbA=">nasacpp.org</a>).
 The student engineer will participate in the NASA CPP Business Startup BSP program on an industrial fan design based upon NASA technology (plane wing) that will increase the efficiency and reduce the noise of current fans in the market. NASA-CPP BSP projects
 and its partnership with NASA has won several awards including the Outstanding Partnership Award, Federal Laboratory Consortium Far West Regional 2017. Former students who participated in this program got internships and jobs in top organizations including,
 &nbsp;<b>NASA</b><b><span style="font-size:9.0pt">, JPL, Northrop Grumman,&nbsp;U.S. Air Force</span></b><span style="font-size:9.0pt">, Aerospace Corp., Walt Disney Corporation, Universal Studios, PepsiCo, etc.</span>&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Benefits of getting involved in this program:</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Resume booster: Several of our previous team members got full time jobs and/or internships at&nbsp;NASA<span style="font-size:9.0pt">,&nbsp;JPL,&nbsp;Northrop Grumman, U.S. Air Force, Aerospace Corp., Walt Disney Corporation, Universal Studios, PepsiCo,
 DHL, Southern California Edison, Kaiser Permanente, Advanced Sterilization Products, Citi National Bank, Enterprise, and Extron Electronics</span>.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Course credit: You can receive 4 units of course credit per quarter. In some cases, this may count as a graduation project. (currently not a paid position)<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Unique Experience: You will gain unique experience in engineering analysis often used in industry, marketing, and entrepreneurship, product pitching (in competitions similar to Shark Tank) by working with cross-functional teams (business,
 engineering, art etc.) &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Responsibilities and Duties</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">The student engineer will be responsible for:<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Attending the weekly NASA-CPP meetings (Fridays 1pm-5pm) to report on weekly progress<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Using Ansys Fluent to simulate flow over the fan blades<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Perform FEA using Ansys or a similar program.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Applying class-learned concepts with aerodynamics of a 3D body<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Developing creative design solutions to improve fan's performance<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Sourcing of manufacturing<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Collaborating with physics, business, and other engineering students<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Design test and procedures for testing<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Preparing reports/documentation/presentations to communicate technical results<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Required Qualifications</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">In order to obtain this position, the engineering student must be:<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Have experience with or willingness to learn Ansys Fluent/FEA analysis<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• familiar with SolidWorks or other similar CAD software<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Studying a related engineering major<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Excellent at written and verbal communication<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• A team player&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Preferred Skills</b><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">It would be preferred for the engineering student to have experience with:<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• A basic understanding of aerodynamics especially pertaining to 3D wing bodies<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Intermediate or advanced knowledge of Ansys&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Graduating Spring 2020 or later<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Knowledge of manufacturing processes<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal">• Experience in machining (CNC, mill, lathe)&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<div>
<div>

<div class="WordSection1">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Dear Electrical Engineering, Computer Engineering, and Engineering Technology students,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">We are looking for a three&nbsp;Electrical/Computer Engineering or Engineering Technology&nbsp;students with a passion for electronics&nbsp;for the NASA-CPP Business Startup Program. &nbsp;Positions are related
 to to rapid prototyping circuits for projects utilizing optical fibers.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">The NASA-CPP Business Startup Program is a Cal Poly Pomona sponsored organization that commercializes NASA technology as well as our own innovative ideas. The program has won several grants
 and awards, including the Outstanding Partnership Award,&nbsp;Federal Laboratory Consortium&nbsp;Far West Regional, Bronco Startup Challenge, and President’s Discovery Fellowship Award. We are starting right away this semester, so applicants are asked to apply immediately
 to be involved as soon as possible.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Benefits of getting involved in this program:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Resume booster: Several of our previous team members got full time jobs and/or internships at NASA, JPL, Northrop Grumman, U.S. Air Force, Aerospace Corp., Walt
 Disney Corporation, Universal Studios, PepsiCo, DHL, Southern California Edison, Kaiser Permanente, Johnson and Johnson, Citi National Bank, Enterprise, and Extron Electronics.</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Course credit: You can receive 4 units of business course credit per semester.&nbsp;<br>
• A &quot;Learn by Doing&quot; approach to developing your technical skills</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Unique Experience: You will gain unique experience in engineering analysis often used in industry, marketing, and entrepreneurship, product pitching (in competitions
 similar to Shark Tank) by working with cross-functional teams (business, engineering, art etc.)&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Responsibilities and Duties:</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">The student engineers will be responsible for:</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Circuit design and implementation as printed circuit boards (PCBs)</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Attending the weekly NASA-CPP meetings (Fridays at 2:30PM) to report on weekly progress</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Develop, and construct prototypes as needed for related projects&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Sourcing of manufacturing</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Collaborating with physics, business, and other engineering students</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Design test and procedures for testing</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">• Preparing reports/documentation/presentations to communicate technical results</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:12.65pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
</div>

------------ Message 72 ------------
To comply with CSU security policies and standards, Cal Poly Pomona requires
all account holders to change their BroncoPasswords on a regular basis. For
more information on University Password Management rules, please see

	https://cpp.service-now.com/ehelp?id=kb_article&sys_id=071fc54e6fe8e600e020f35d5d3ee4c1

BroncoPasswords are used for most common online applications such as
BroncoDirect/PeopleSoft and Blackboard.

You are receiving this notice because the BroncoPassword for account
cjkeenan will expire on September 21, 2018.

For uninterrupted access, you must set a new BroncoPassword before the current
one expires.

	To change your BroncoPassword, please
	-	Go to the CPP home page (http://www.cpp.edu)
	-	Click on the "Change Your Password" link
		at the bottom of the page

Any programs or devices that store your BroncoPassword will need to be updated
with your new BroncoPassword. 

If you have any questions, please contact the Cal Poly Pomona IT Service Desk
at (909) 869.6776 or send e-mail to itservicedesk@cpp.edu. Our office hours
are Monday - Thursday from 7:30 am to 6:00 pm and Friday from 8:00 am to 5:00
pm, excluding state holidays. Please don't send us your password by email -
you need to keep it secure, even from us!

Cal Poly Pomona IT Service Desk

<p class="MsoNormal">Dear Engineering Students,<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">The College of Business invites you to attend their LinkedIn networking workshop.
<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b>Using LinkedIn for Career Development Workshop</b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Wednesday, September 19, 2018<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">6 p.m. to 7:30 p.m.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Bronco Student Center, Ursa Major<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">To register, visit: <span style="color:#1F497D"><a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcbaalumnilinkedinfall.eventbrite.com&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7Cae48946c780a4e4a337208d61a9780e0%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636725635507863206&amp;sdata=8YHigM8SISShWD3AL4ttu1FVnczz%2BkJo7gGJ43HA4Fo%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="https://cbaalumnilinkedinfall.eventbrite.com" shash="YtGboQrfX8FPMdAchxsoCEFNvlL3EJrKEPdla6whienfP5X8UGyhXt6P7V&#43;TjKhdeXFWrG/JDon3nWwwmms0wclBnRqrB&#43;wcGIjU8ubqadLOVeb146m&#43;LXT0dTQdZjOFJZyn&#43;3J3nFtPdFNn8Fhr1wA9wsnPYlnftoWotBoqE/8="><span style="color:#0563C1">https://cbaalumnilinkedinfall.eventbrite.com</span></a></span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Light refreshments will be served.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i>&nbsp;</i><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i>Business professional attire recommended! You will have the opportunity to have a professional photo taken of you and meet with industry professionals.</i><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">In this session, industry professionals guide you through LinkedIn’s ins and outs and the useful tools that it provides you when trying to establish your professional network. We strongly encourage you to attend as this session will provide
 knowledge and insight on how to establish good professional connections in industry.<o:p></o:p></p>

<div class="WordSection1">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;line-height:115%"><b>The new Fire Safety Report is now available:
</b><a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~housing/Documents/fire_safety_report1.pdf">You may view or download the report by clicking on this link</a><u><span style="color:#0563C1"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;line-height:115%">Per the Code of Federal Regulations, Institutional Fire Safety Policies and Fire Statistics, 34 CFR 668.49(b), any institution that maintains an on-campus housing facility must collect fire
 statistics, publish an Annual Fire Safety Report, and keep a &#8220;fire log.&#8221; <o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;line-height:115%">The purpose of the Fire Safety Report is to disclose fire safety policies and procedures related to our on-campus student housing and to disclose statistics for fires that occurred in these
 facilities.&nbsp; Cal Poly Pomona&#8217;s Fire Safety Report provides this information for University Housing Services and Foundation Housing Services/University Village.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;line-height:115%">The Fire Safety Report includes the following components:
<o:p></o:p></p>
<ol style="margin-top:0in" start="1" type="1">
<li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Description of each on-campus student housing facility fire safety system <o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Number of fire drills held during the previous calendar year<o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Policies or rules on portable electrical appliances, smoking, and open flames in a student housing facility<o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Procedures for evacuation in case of fire<o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Policies regarding fire safety education and training programs, <o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
A list of the titles of each person or organization to which students and employees should report that a fire in on-campus student housing occurred.
<o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Plans for future improvements in fire safety<o:p></o:p></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:12.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
Fire statistics for the previous three calendar years<o:p></o:p></li></ol>
<p class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;mso-add-space:auto;line-height:115%">
<span style="color:#1F497D"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:10.0pt;line-height:115%">To request a print copy of the 2018 Fire Safety Report, contact the University Housing Services Office in Building 59 or Foundation Housing Services/University Village at 3400 Poly Vista Building
 300, Pomona.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class="MsoNormal">Hello Engineering <span style="color:#1F497D">S</span>tudents<span style="color:#1F497D">,</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">I&#8217;m happy to share with you a new leadership opportunity for engineering students that I hope you will consider as part of your education here at Cal Poly Pomona. Employers often tell us they are looking for graduates with technical skills
 as well as leadership qualities, which can be further cultivated through participation in clubs, events, and now through the Engineering Student Ambassador program.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">The College of Engineering Student Ambassador Program is a leadership opportunity for engineering students who are dedicated to representing Cal Poly Pomona College of Engineering. Engineering Student Ambassadors (ESAs) are a select group
 of undergraduate students who possess leadership qualities, have a passion for the College of Engineering, STEAM education and Cal Poly Pomona. The ESAs serve as motivated liaisons of the College of Engineering on and off-campus.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">I invite you to read about the benefits of becoming an ESA, the qualifications, and find the application form at
<b><span style="color:#2F5597;mso-style-textfill-fill-color:#2F5597;mso-style-textfill-fill-alpha:100.0%"><a href="http://www.cpp.edu/~engineering/ESA/Join.shtml"><span style="color:#2F5597;mso-style-textfill-fill-color:#2F5597;mso-style-textfill-fill-alpha:100.0%">http://www.cpp.edu/~engineering/ESA/Join.shtml</span></a></span></b>.
 &nbsp;If you are interested in this highly competitive opportunity, please be sure to visit the website and submit an application by the deadline of Friday, October 12, 2018, and interviews will be held in the fall semester. I look forward to seeing our new ESAs
 proudly representing the College of Engineering very soon!<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Go Broncos!<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Regards,<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Hello Engineering Students!<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">The Southern California Engineering Technologists Association (SCETA) will be hosting our second general meeting of the 2018-2019 academic year
 this upcoming Thursday. We will be talking about some important topics pertaining to CES as well as what is coming up.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">The upcoming meeting will be held on:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Date:&nbsp;<span style="background:yellow">Thursday October 4<sup>th</sup>, 2018</span></span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Time:&nbsp;<span style="background:yellow">U-Hour (12:00 PM – 12:50 PM)</span></span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Where:&nbsp;<span style="background:yellow">Building 9, Room 247</span>&nbsp;(Across from the Electro-Mechanical Engineering Technology department office)</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">*LIMITED free food will be provided, but paid members will have priority first.</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Three key topics we will be discussing:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">1.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">SCETA Membership - $30, we will be accepting payment at the end of this
 meeting!<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">a.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Includes 2 free shirts<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">b.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Opportunities to go to CES 2019 and factory tours<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">c.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Socials hosted by SCETA<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">d.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Free food at our general meetings all year long<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">2.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">CES 2019<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">a.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Updates on process<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">b.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Google form to sign up:&nbsp;<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2Fforms%2FARWkfjL3PLvYDA5l1&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7Cbfb4e662d6c04d68d71c08d62898d842%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636741034287186822&amp;sdata=EZCdoApOEho7tjSLy2ER71fZre8d4gx0RjyGJIGvVmo%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="https://goo.gl/forms/ARWkfjL3PLvYDA5l1" shash="C6WZ0Iu6u2mY33YEHYIpI9bWOBTK7OKBqT&#43;zsjlglJqwrbdHP5tLPoAQBa/rRAAjDu3NubELHEX6/7A0przKNkQa&#43;ctiA8bZQyE17vqs9A60ZF1WKqQuIA/d9&#43;79E8OS4PV8DEti4h/RPuPytl9tTNSbSSiNZQT&#43;NzNaR1UyB1s="><span style="color:#0563C1">https://goo.gl/forms/ARWkfjL3PLvYDA5l1</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">3.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Round 1 Social<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="gmail-msolistparagraph" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:11.75pt">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">a.</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Thursday, October 11<sup>th</sup>&nbsp;@ 7:00 PM<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">*If you are interested in any of these topics, it is&nbsp;<b><u>HIGHLY recommended</u></b>&nbsp;you attend the upcoming Thursday meeting as our club will
 be hosting them.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:11.75pt"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;">Feel free to stop by during our meeting to see what we have to offer. We hope to see you at the meeting! If you have any more questions you can
 bring them up at the meeting or contact me at&nbsp;<span class="gmail-msohyperlink"><span style="color:#0563C1"><a href="mailto:sceta.secretary@gmail.com"><span style="color:#0563C1">sceta.secretary@gmail.com</span></a></span></span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Dear College of Engineering Students<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;outline: 0px;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;orphans: 2;text-align:start;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;word-spacing:0px">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Here is an update on upcoming events and workshops happening at MEP:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<div align="center" style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:center">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">
<hr size="2" width="100%" align="center">
</span></div>
<p style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;outline: 0px;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;orphans: 2;text-align:start;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;word-spacing:0px">
<b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">MEP U-Hour workshops:<br>
</span></b><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Full Calendar Link:&nbsp;<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdrive.google.com%2Fopen%3Fid%3D109XdZuryb5iJTK9Z1_UsJOOSqRQHTDrC&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C0f93c09c009d480639ce08d62b168917%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636743781705389171&amp;sdata=87x1wzYnfgb%2BEJ8I7akeIUGrDtzLvy7pZE7zXk7B8nM%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="https://drive.google.com/open?id=109XdZuryb5iJTK9Z1_UsJOOSqRQHTDrC" shash="xqdOnIhqtpGM3mg7MDwxJDFLhrNpwsWt/aGChAUtoUGD96uqKHydYapR3&#43;jfqjloQNE5oBzkAt3NYM/dQsUdjLuqd/xdFrp3oe3Rl7/isEjv44LalIYlg&#43;RpgzP8udlNQAHWCz9iGt56jpi&#43;3iP&#43;o6GFPh/wvhQ9/gGjfTkqITU=" target="_blank"><span style="color:#00748B;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">https://drive.google.com/open?id=109XdZuryb5iJTK9Z1_UsJOOSqRQHTDrC</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p style="mso-margin-top-alt:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.0pt;margin-left:0in;outline: 0px;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;orphans: 2;text-align:start;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;word-spacing:0px">
<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Please click on a link to register!&nbsp; Limit 35 students per session!<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK198"></a><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Hey Bronco,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Last week, we sent you
</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif"><a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fbit.ly%2F2PrGxqA&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C8cffe8ed16fa4720c42508d62eeda6dd%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636748004568514452&amp;sdata=c%2F3W3E9YEyAxmPlNLne4Fl1atef0djGZ8imleqmpLO8%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://bit.ly/2PrGxqA" shash="pbfNr39sRkyP8Bhjp30MX6gls6Rv585/6OzH2tyAGOGQdbeu94wH2c6PKN8uv2JxNQOEdmyrFElSQw90DDjEtmcuFqfWmp66f3CuYFz3IWBbOKIPV3LDiRDq8zGQmXm7dpZx48OdttZ9X&#43;zrMv&#43;BhhvNfA1fS9xJU5R0YxeWmxM=" originalsrc="http://bit.ly/2PrGxqA" shash="q52YwB3ajQZW9/kvQHgSQGZdka&#43;eHweV8hcoQ3FN9QiCruw2aj7LAuZeU0hAhNk06VKHypvz0xx&#43;7EiUPlESqHY4yxW5x/U0WLN9GaVorLhivyAIzOKlqsPZrqd4dxpPx/l77how2JYwA6hwYFFCsSpuX&#43;8D/DlQq8iOGFpdPyI=">a
 message</a><span style="color:black"> with tips on how to get ready for&nbsp;spring 2019 registration. Priority registration is October 17 &amp; 18, and general registration starts on October 22.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Here are the next three tips to help you get ready to register:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Check your holds, and read the hold details.</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Some holds can prevent you from registering, so take care of any holds you have now. You can check your holds in the upper right hand corner of your
<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dirbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fmy.cpp.edu%252F&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C8cffe8ed16fa4720c42508d62eeda6dd%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636748004568524457&amp;sdata=V3RUoISZ28qXfp964YWv7TFs5XvCSz36Df65Inpk2b0%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fmy.cpp.edu%2F" shash="ZVsN9ZNOlBlaZNp31RcdBZE59Ydp92W4PZxDf0R4YhMoUBp&#43;YvkrVggFuWvE6xpmRIBKq5ZmSic80RmS3Xwe5gQcDhzIL9dRJ4nBuIGmzIKXobYAeI7gEjtIdHRjEJ6f7uGV&#43;xHw3/M309W4xikMBevzkcWfkVQVrNTWaS7tR3k=" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fmy.cpp.edu%2F" shash="XGgL/Y3UUOfMMz/fgKfOlOKUIjGNvDXZPmGb8S73QbBRMLkFiFdbNO0x22fjtC/Ar5ex87udFnblCGWX2ZGXzwK2zSwUNW9sqOsJhpwhAku82ajanO9C7l233PDVUVzDeICUN4BWSlI3XxgmVJdkjxlkOgOWhS7tBZzRxdLY4fI=" target="_blank">
Student Center</a>.&nbsp;Remember, some holds -- like Math and English placement holds -- are informational and do not prevent you from registering.
<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dirbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.youtube.com%252Fwatch%253Fv%253DDylhQNDOuCQ&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C8cffe8ed16fa4720c42508d62eeda6dd%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636748004568524457&amp;sdata=oHtR24TM9oSN%2F22hazXpM0pgwKSz%2BBJ46eoizs42VsE%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DDylhQNDOuCQ" shash="MnwWRtQVQq1//khPeaByq1uo9fEropro8KenIxaKB9fG2Lguv6nZc/zAr5mo6ZvoV4gTX0piKy2dgUdGpQ9PU&#43;ftTmVIqEJHdaLO6gc&#43;Fb7dT9F4WDhhBtBS7HwMEpFPDCpPMpgdz/mR0GeGdRmGnCN3JBP7zH124oHapOaV8o8=" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DDylhQNDOuCQ" shash="jT5R1ENjiA61vlKS4nDAxt23gbxFQ6ayQXBowhqW41MdBc5XZdNmSO4OndyqWMXvxoT&#43;b/mn&#43;VXha95GXjywAZeC5CF9SgjN8FJF7lyeKWg5PbgdcQuV6NbfCwSWdH9Pu80JTQP&#43;et27O4FZNaccDsAHenyOEHbfDzsjQ1xBAFw=" target="_blank">
Read the details of the hold</a> by clicking on the Holds link to see if they prevent you from registering.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Use your academic planning tools.&nbsp;</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dirbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fadvising%252Findex.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C8cffe8ed16fa4720c42508d62eeda6dd%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636748004568534461&amp;sdata=XgyrlBNpxeiSSyT%2FDEQw%2BB0uQFJW%2Ba7KOtXyAC0T7ms%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fadvising%2Findex.shtml" shash="KtR&#43;dArBlGk0S89KDCAexVS/OzQ0b/ZdHdweQ4HVRNVxoL0QvrtPodDh40I&#43;rKHer8tddnGFo24uuajlDXhKk3IZm8jtBGxiOWKb4z/PA0bnQohxE2QNrbxZ2cMpRSEuU/w2D6J/13F3FFlI4T1LAjATaPQF4ThMCi&#43;XEM90ugE=" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fadvising%2Findex.shtml" shash="rMiy5/yX3G/7PevgHrw8uMBh&#43;pzzSHXo6pHvao4m2x30fb2XcEXhIpk6N1tXY05tVcx60HQtHnkbvcmJTRGcmKSHp9pDv&#43;jPHZG2Q09Xax76cTBX2OrBdnLE/aBep4Uef&#43;znJeGX6D&#43;qRiysFmLP&#43;jCujzQLZVSwrnZ/WZA8zHY=" target="_blank">Student
 Success Central's Advising &amp; Academic Resources page</a>&nbsp;gives you an entire list of what's in your academic planning toolbox, including links to curriculum sheets, MyPlanner resources and General Education listings. If you're transitioning from quarter to
 semesters, continue to use the Course Conversion Guide, the quarter-to-semester General Education tool and your other Semester Conversion resources.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Use the Registration Guide.&nbsp;</span></strong><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">The
<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dirbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fguides%252Fregistration%252Findex.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C8cffe8ed16fa4720c42508d62eeda6dd%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636748004568534461&amp;sdata=DA9COW3uLBOJ%2FbweebFvjLmQ1L6b1i6Fuds6At%2FFeFg%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fguides%2Fregistration%2Findex.shtml" shash="yzkh52HU00P1PIny0GwpsWh8Ctrww3L1QPANugJPA9mKNETOm0hBgMtDq/UW14Nubuy4i5hOmaFQ4MNCPn&#43;hmJ3j6SPR/kDMC0uwT2w7oYOgEtsp9&#43;IsIiqWeUhl9jt44qt7paSLdhFboq5&#43;T9cRP1sximyqtyqPwu2oqC&#43;xgq8=" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fguides%2Fregistration%2Findex.shtml" shash="BQr/18gVgu0c9dT1opI&#43;PQnscGj5RDyK9myFM21DnTsQgsnSK6&#43;inySydMWWgKjF0B5gcR0W5igK58hgul/KbGlnkXrCPL6oH0VEPipxFWXF197K/XKEtIfvDhlKSEH4TsDBvIAMjLDHB/PE7UP53p0rYuknbep83sMrdf7tfeE=" target="_blank">
Student Success Central Registration Guide</a> walks you through what to do before, during and after registration. Read through it to refresh your memory.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">At any point throughout registration, feel free to reach out to the
<a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dirbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fbac%252Findex.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7C%7C8cffe8ed16fa4720c42508d62eeda6dd%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636748004568544470&amp;sdata=nFpTXG%2FKEIChpUTIjibkAuowcs5jwPflGvioWhyLWag%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fbac%2Findex.shtml" shash="qOgafG9er8PMKqQEV5qeiCTHdeNUCrASk6i&#43;ohZMwd417YKEIbt8xCPgKzj/0xbTTOCbqqaoYmwQzeH6EWpch2jfvTIPijESBUO2qC1sQoKNHuL/QjwBq1VoqHEIbFVW2U/C7bMgX8VGSd/IUEEt87XjzEcKe2xkVCWGmUDaSzA=" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=irbv8q6ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fbac%2Findex.shtml" shash="t/7kautgYdIDfxzdHrKngMwdW4bbhRO9qKO/4YVsIKajhr1acEQCwUPbR2yxgsnSScw1lYHdx/UiaIBNfvMWUuQknBM1KQbGW/eARqcN0RhDQ52mrRxXFuT1kHSsFtz6LBZ4nT6KiPOKqJN4lDy80hTti4eIMSj6iOUvQSc0tFk=" target="_blank">
Bronco Advising Center</a> to ask questions and get help. We'll be back next week with your last tips.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

------------ Message 123 ------------
To comply with CSU security policies and standards, Cal Poly Pomona requires
all account holders to change their BroncoPasswords on a regular basis. For
more information on University Password Management rules, please see

	https://cpp.service-now.com/ehelp?id=kb_article&sys_id=071fc54e6fe8e600e020f35d5d3ee4c1

BroncoPasswords are used for most common online applications such as
BroncoDirect/PeopleSoft and Blackboard.

You are receiving this notice because the BroncoPassword for account
cjkeenan will expire on May 31, 2019.

For uninterrupted access, you must set a new BroncoPassword before the current
one expires.

	To change your BroncoPassword, please
	-	Go to the CPP home page (http://www.cpp.edu)
	-	Click on the "Change Your Password" link
		at the bottom of the page

Any programs or devices that store your BroncoPassword will need to be updated
with your new BroncoPassword. 

If you have any questions, please contact the Cal Poly Pomona IT Service Desk
at (909) 869.6776 or send e-mail to itservicedesk@cpp.edu. Our office hours
are Monday - Thursday from 7:30 am to 6:00 pm and Friday from 8:00 am to 5:00
pm, excluding state holidays. Please don't send us your password by email -
you need to keep it secure, even from us!

Cal Poly Pomona IT Service Desk

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif">We invite you to take a moment to provide your voice with the following 5 minute survey on the Focus on Finals initiative that took place on campus from May 6 – May 17.
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif">Your feedback is needed to further assess your needs during pre-finals and finals week, and gives you an opportunity to share your thoughts and concerns.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Participation is completely voluntary, and your responses are anonymous.
</span><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:#C00000">At the end of the survey, you will have the option of providing your name and Bronco ID, which will be entered into a drawing for a chance to win a BroncoBucks gift card.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:#C00000"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Take the Survey:
<b><a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fbaseline.campuslabs.com%2Fcpp%2Ffocusonfinals&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C4109ce6f0207454fd15a08d6db1a2d06%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C636939770712151789&amp;sdata=QANXl3d2Z8np6AqvHTSBV8W5U6X4w8s7s1EbM7eNgLY%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="https://baseline.campuslabs.com/cpp/focusonfinals" shash="ZCPoMg14zp0hBKNi1cN/Nglt5U/HjKUXy7kutfCcJPGdYjbGeat4Kbq12UdkrIy0eEm&#43;jnYhYE5FiMBHZT&#43;TI8SU1SxNb3tg3sZokka6/zlvZ9vWLMsuUkAt9A8Jdcof6fZEjJj1j51Jd64stT4lDmZOXWtqoLThQ2NqrNr&#43;Dbs="><span style="color:black">https://baseline.campuslabs.com/cpp/focusonfinals</span></a></b><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<body lang="EN-US" link="#0563C1" vlink="#954F72">
<div class="WordSection1">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Dear Members of the Campus Community,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Effective today, July 1, 2019, at 5 PM, the Division of Information Technology &amp; Institutional Planning (IT&amp;IP) is implementing a new trial email
 feature to assist with our email information security efforts. <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-bottom:2.0pt"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Email messages that are received by members of the Cal Poly Pomona community that are sent by individuals or organizations outside of our immediate community,
 will be labeled as “external” in the following manner:&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul style="margin-top:0in" type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top:2.0pt;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-add-space:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-size:12.0pt">“[EXTERNAL]” added to the beginning of the subject line<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-add-space:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-size:12.0pt">A banner added to the top of the message body that reads:
<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<div style="border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:1.0pt 4.0pt 1.0pt 4.0pt">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:3.0pt;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;margin-left:.5in">
<span style="font-size:12.0pt">“<b><span style="color:#860038">CAUTION:</span></b>&nbsp;This email was not sent from a Cal Poly Pomona service. Exercise caution when clicking links or opening attachments.”&nbsp;
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">We are hoping these labels will assist the campus community in identifying fraudulent emails and provide reminders to use extra caution when opening emails from unknown individuals.
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">When a message is labeled as “external”, you should exercise additional caution:&nbsp;
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul style="margin-top:0in" type="disc">
<li class="xmsonormal" style="mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><i><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Verify email addresses before sending or replying-to an “external” email</span></i><span style="font-size:12.0pt">.&nbsp;&nbsp; If you feel the message is suspicious, directly verify
 with the reported sender using another communication method that the message is legitimate prior to taking any action.&nbsp;
<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="xmsonormal" style="mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><i><span style="font-size:12.0pt;background:white">Think before you act:</span></i><span style="font-size:12.0pt;background:white">&nbsp; Be suspicious of communication that requests immediate action, asks you
 to spend money, offers something that sounds too good to be true or asks for personal information.&nbsp;
</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="xmsonormal" style="mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><i><span style="font-size:12.0pt;background:white">Report suspicious emails to the division</span></i><span style="font-size:12.0pt;background:white">.&nbsp; To report a suspicious message to a member of the
 information security team, send a copy of the message, as an email attachment if possible, to<i>
</i></span><a href="mailto:suspectemail@cpp.edu"><i><span style="font-size:12.0pt;background:white">suspectemail@cpp.edu</span></i></a><i><span style="font-size:12.0pt;background:white">.
</span></i><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="xmsonormal" style="mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">To report an email that is part of the campus community that has been incorrectly labeled as external, please send an email to
</span><a href="mailto:suspectemail@cpp.edu"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">suspectemail@cpp.edu</span></a><span style="font-size:12.0pt">.
<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Note: If you utilize Outlook “Rules” to handle messages based on the subject line, you may need to update your rules to account for the “[EXTERNAL]”
 tag that will be added to the subject line.&nbsp; If you do not use “Rules”, then changes are not needed.&nbsp;
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">We are expecting to operate this trial for approximately 45-60 days and make enhancements to this email security feature based on campus feedback.
 For additional questions and feedback regarding email security, contact the campus CISO at
</span><a href="mailto:ciso@cpp.edu"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">ciso@cpp.edu</span></a><span style="font-size:12.0pt">.&nbsp; For questions regarding the use of campus email, contact the IT Service Desk at

------------ Message 133 ------------
Dear All, 

I am traveling to Austin, Tx for presenting my research paper on low-power reconfigurable architecture for securing small devices. ﻿﻿﻿﻿﻿﻿﻿﻿For this coming Monday, there will no be a lecture. Instead, I want you guys to work on selecting the course project and finalize the list of members per group. We are in total 34, which means every group should be five members except one would be just four members. The list of project topics are the following:
1) Lightweight cryptography security of small devices. It is a competition sponsored by the National Institute of Standard and Technology NIST for securing small devices. There are 56 submissions for the first round. Each submission has two algorithms. The first algorithm is a lightweight hash function with different sizes and the second algorithm is a lightweight block cipher. Every submission included in their packages a reference code  (C language-based). What I want you to think about is the following:
1.a) implement one of the algorithms on FPGA using the concept of RISC architecture. 
2.a) check all the possible performance metrics we are learning on your implementation and spell it out in the scientific paper you will submit as a final report
3.a) create a GitHub per group and upload all your work materials there 
4.a) create a QR-code connected to your GitHub and distribute on all possible companies as a part of finding a job after the graduation

For your reference,  the link of the competition is https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcsrc.nist.gov%2FProjects%2FLightweight-Cryptography%2Fround-1-candidates&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7Cd8fbaf3af535411cb43808d7334a3494%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637034266126803721&amp;sdata=92lVaz%2FJiJ8BbRhvlEZQlgsACOumNLEULkwf4fQwf3s%3D&amp;reserved=0 

2) you can pick up one of the lightweight cryptography algorithms and implement on different embedded systems platforms and also do profiling, which means find the performance metrics like the size of memory usage, power consumption, TFLOPS, and MIPS metrics,.etc  
Try to check Amdhal law concept in step 1 and 2 

Another possible project
Find one of the CNN neural networks for audio, text, image, or video recognition and implement on FPGA with measuring the performance metrics (Execution time, CPI, .....) 

Another possible project
run a benchmark as Chai or SPEC2008 on your own RISC Implementation with checking all the performance metrics
Another potential project
Pick up one of the computer vision algorithms and adapt it on FPGA with doing performance metrics study 

Another possible project
Pick up one of the video compression algorithms and adapt it on FPGA with doing performance metrics study  

Another possible project
Bring your project with justifying the novelty and what scientific way you will follow to measure the performance of the project from the computer architecture perspective.

On Wednesday: Professor El-Naga will give you a lecture on the performance metrics, and from there, I will continue with you after I back from the conference. 

Please don't hesitate to contact me if you have any questions or concerns!
Have a wonderful weekend!
Kind regards, 
Mohamed


------------ Message 134 ------------
Dear All, 
Regarding the task, I gave you which involving PLL. 
You should know PLL  means Phase-Locked Loop. There is no straightforward IP called PLL. You have to go to the IP catalog and choose the clock wizard, and from there you will find one of the options PLL. You will find a couple of taps for input clock, output clocks. If you remember, I asked for 32 different clocks. You can have a couple of PLL and take from the output, or you can cascade them our you can choose from them a tree of clocks. I give you the full freedom to pick up the right setup be sure to justify your choices in a one-page report withdrawing the circuit I gave it to you. I would like to see the design on-chip running next time we will meet. 

For lecture two material, I am going to upload it now. 

All the best, 
Have a nice weekend!
Mohamed

<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdrive.google.com%2Fopen%3Fid%3D1smjPgRx5vPfjQYC99ULafR-7CAchQaN_&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7Ccf65122e24a2411060c108d74469d1dc%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637053093585593947&amp;sdata=YdSZZqRK5ah1YpBTM%2FVKXzUcvpg2ou%2Fy7FqnAE83wZA%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="https://drive.google.com/open?id=1smjPgRx5vPfjQYC99ULafR-7CAchQaN_" shash="Mu28qNJcDNtdh&#43;Qw55lku43O16DaOExjfkafgxAI9h&#43;ICh/OAuhbehDDW8C9iJOuM4be2nN0Ac3a5tb4sUTbpOoaz5MRfyke4V4kxMfhazCZVVeOOcHfYvwANcPLSo3dsbiZjw6pPs4xAR9BuRrBrkuCvWojfDcEgPuA8FOzpws=" originalsrc="https://drive.google.com/open?id=1smjPgRx5vPfjQYC99ULafR-7CAchQaN_" shash="bjl8zMJ41u5DRTlswslHvPTsXc1AtdXxKaMnWnVT6qfGQVuH1GCGjC4YkKI09NO7htdRyP83c50KBZOpTZKqovJx5Wkd7GedVmi/J83VOgjT/gVIcfUjftQ45nltpYWJcfmcABn&#43;K9Svrrnp6mzglFnV2ICM6LVhuknknG7Jx2o=" id="LPlnk830703" class="">https://drive.google.com/open?id=1smjPgRx5vPfjQYC99ULafR-7CAchQaN_</a></div>
<div style="font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-family: Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;" class="">
<br class="">
</div>
<div style="font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-family: Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;" class="">
Currently we are in decent shape - we have a good portion of the parts already, and in the next week I intend to get the board, 14 gauge wire, etc itself so we can start adding components.</div>
<div style="font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-family: Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;" class="">
Jacob picked up the relays we need to actuate on the board, and we intend to display the status of each length of 'transmission line' using LED strings, with the color representing where power is being routed around.</div>
<div style="font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-family: Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;" class="">
<br class="">
</div>
<div style="font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-family: Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;" class="">
In the next ~week to 10 days the following things should happen.</div>
<div style="font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-family: Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;" class="">
<ol class="">
<li class="">Andrew is going to upload the one-line diagram for the overall behavior of the system</li><li class="">I'll upload the physical design/electrical design drafts for the specific connection points (when/where/why)</li><li class="">Jacob will upload a mostly complete parts list with what we have, what we need (sensors, switches, cable-ties, etc)<br class="">
</li></ol>
<div class="">After that the next step is our first attempt to actually assemble the parts, and see what needs to change. (I know something will have to change)</div>
<div class=""><br class="">
</div>
<div class="">I have a loose expectation that we can start playing with trying to get actual data out of the build by the last week of October, at which point we would be transitioning to some of the 2nd phase goals, where our system actually has to do something
 to respond to our faults.</div>
<div class=""><br class="">
</div>
<div class="">If you have any questions, feel free to let me know and I'll find out what I can. Enjoy your weekend.</div>
<div class=""><br class="">
</div>
<div class="">Respectfully,</div>
<div class=""><br class="">
</div>
<div class="">Dennis P. Getsie Jr.</div>
</div>

<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK198"></a><span style="display:none"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<div align="center">
<table class="MsoNormalTable" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="width:100.0%;display:table" id="content_LETTER.BLOCK198">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="padding:5.25pt 6.0pt 5.25pt 6.0pt">
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Hey Bronco,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">It's almost time for spring 2020 registration! Priority registration is October 14 and 15, and general registration starts on October 16.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Over the next few weeks we'll be sending you messages with tips on how to get ready. Here are the first tips:&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">You have a specific enrollment appointment.</span></strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Enrollment appointments, or the day and time you can begin to register, are set by your class standing and the amount of units you've
<strong><u><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">completed:</span></u></strong> not what you're projected to complete with your fall 2019 classes. Your appointment will be assigned closer to when registration begins.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">The Registrar's Office will schedule several days between each class standing's enrollment appointment to&nbsp;ease the strain on BroncoDirect and give you more time to ask questions&nbsp;before
 the next group of students register. Your appointment may be a little later in the general registration period, but this should not affect class availability.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Fill out your MyPlanner, and see your academic advisor.</span></strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Your MyPlanner not only helps you and your advisor keep track of what you want to take, but tells your department what you want to take and in what term.&nbsp;Watch
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dtzpdko4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.youtube.com%252Fwatch%253Fv%253D3-jk-ddRbiA&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7Cf6efbe97e6b549ef9adc08d74814a37f%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637057139213652528&amp;sdata=HMgytNq8I26yCpl92eivjriffyFxpRO2JOnrgWNiErk%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=tzpdko4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D3-jk-ddRbiA" shash="nKsbBjpUrcWIGMHBGiHe5DBfaSFFvHip4ZmoLpe11moA/ttjCwbxi5OgLy0lYejkASFA/1mh/enWOTpo7&#43;7ILx9VJIZm8CnJyeYPK5yA/3izgWvxBcCW1aqMhUP&#43;mXH0wc1RN1g9QIGNO7MMPRMdEh5LIE8LMRoOB/9/L4RRrMY=" target="_blank">
this how-to video</a> if you're not sure of how to update it.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Use the
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dtzpdko4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fdirectories%252Fadvising-directory.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7Cf6efbe97e6b549ef9adc08d74814a37f%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637057139213652528&amp;sdata=4R8t6aHNLvTCqj42d2rsfy%2BcJ4Q0JFQQe%2F2bNCt4zbE%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=tzpdko4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fdirectories%2Fadvising-directory.shtml" shash="wgFoCYb34uEm9bQyVYi14G&#43;QjWUjEHr14o59PDnhXmJRInetEMLhL0J3Q0&#43;v8PHL64Myw1Sr8Dju&#43;KMYjOhQne4VKu3PDHgo7koj59aST8Ul/XknDkSPJgMjRqRVPMHm9vvpJ9tWypaJOec8t&#43;4SZpl8GjI2Dr2PZsSyBK4sS6c=" target="_blank">
Advising Directory</a> on Student Success Central to help you find your college advising center. If you're unsure of who your advisor is, reach out to the
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dtzpdko4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fbac%252Findex.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7Cf6efbe97e6b549ef9adc08d74814a37f%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637057139213662521&amp;sdata=KwJW5Fgz0yxR5kyvD11uUVhUy5uHdn43ZnIPQtDgx1I%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=tzpdko4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fbac%2Findex.shtml" shash="P98nRwB0e1dXiGkC3erzCFlv&#43;pEFHYAZQJhqNWggnOJPCrCXCRMuoWnXCugnsRQKO0kKJZtZN4IbsS&#43;VnpuqbwGcLCf/OtoU7sKThwZh5YYYdX9wVfg9XhNkMMiga/rJzsqTIKUxRTcV&#43;v4meoeMVwRx4qClBjztGE8K&#43;&#43;vZP&#43;k=" target="_blank">
Bronco Advising Center</a>. We'll help you find their contact information.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Plan for 30 semester units across the academic year.</span></strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Most undergraduate degrees at Cal Poly Pomona requires 120 semester units. If you want to graduate in two (for transfer students) or four years (for freshmen), planning for 30
 units keeps you on track to do that.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Visit the

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><u><span style="font-size:11.5pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif;color:#203864">CSS’s Mission Statement</span></u></b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:11.5pt;font-family:&quot;Helvetica&quot;,sans-serif;color:#203864;background:white">CSS is a place for students with interests in technology as it pertains to software to meet up and learn more about the field. Students learn
 from other like-minded students and from the many visiting guest speakers on topics that are current and relevant to the industry. Topics often include software development, programming languages, game development, operating systems and many other topics both
 big and small. We will also be hosting events, seminars, and workshops outside of regular meeting so stay tuned!
</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Regards, <o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><a name="LETTER.BLOCK198"></a><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Hey Bronco,<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<div>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">We wanted to check in with you after the first few weeks of general registration, and offer some tips and strategies to help you finalize your spring 2020 schedule.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
<ul type="disc">

<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fcpp.az1.qualtrics.com%252Fjfe%252Fform%252FSV_9N21UuuhA36TaIZ&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138649222&amp;sdata=xluKpyHcRvYwifcaOeWCpF1NZ2qKXEHD2YTLwhGaI%2FM%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fcpp.az1.qualtrics.com%2Fjfe%2Fform%2FSV_9N21UuuhA36TaIZ" shash="mCr3fZd2UKGfa7o/GGa582eXQrhbebkVc7a1Rb5MEtZ4nf4R2MzteM1Z&#43;I40SxcghHRCqrcEvBoI0UgpB6Bl9OGszctcZbrkXbGjKxGIOdGj6mQQZe93cEizhamngYjX9Qrhfx6SNhqE25TgGrej1WgPYbwM12qsK5c4/mSVkPU=" target="_blank">
short survey</a>, and enter the opportunity drawing for $50 in Bronco Bucks.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
