BroncoDirect Class Search</a> and your <a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fmy.cpp.edu%252F&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138659219&amp;sdata=36yBBvRa4SGkxq7jAo4wpNv2DPd%2BArhOAR8096fhA0U%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fmy.cpp.edu%2F" shash="dqQC7mIhLtTiTwYoNm/iMaXc2G6HdixmLooUSZ2KGzYm3du9j3LRxmixvIP&#43;C4f8d27T8AFLhKvuDqCGwYWc7T3yF8iceooRDoecZljJ8JnI/&#43;6YhXrGIqbDhVVyHFpAw3ATmiJaUmcb0mbGYafxSJtF0EQMCq7Fa3DfutF962Q=" target="_blank">
CPP email</a> to learn when new sections open.<o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">If you have a Title IX hold, you should
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Eofficeofequity%252FtitleIX%252Ftrainings.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138669213&amp;sdata=37tSAqVasnOeiq85LRwkmeVMw087zrbbI787lgXWjjc%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Eofficeofequity%2FtitleIX%2Ftrainings.shtml" shash="Fz8v07aVVdB21ExR78Zyshe71ynC400kvayPSDuBl&#43;JIF3j16ovFQ4IjbNMHQNKe3e6Ef/6jfLXxXArzKnmZ5cSnXK9UWETar4UGywNnM0/FoarVOPGHnDslELj3E8FSjnNcBCI0F/Uxp/4cCFPZY0NJJVBsYoBc2zntNNInMNA=" target="_blank">
complete the training</a> ASAP -- the hold will be removed within a few days. If you have an Advising hold, you should meet with your
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fdirectories%252Fadvising-directory.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138669213&amp;sdata=BaIOVX02c1VTwimBSq2YCNp7Kbj%2Bys9rsTzoX4SA%2F6o%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fdirectories%2Fadvising-directory.shtml" shash="fP8GC2c77X6Ytn0ltUnrMQzjRTJvdYsnd5uIgpZu90vSVLWr6SKVk1wGO8XSxhkHTLJlg8ksQfJ/IOD6Pmev9FVCgnywQwezyrxSagPcM96jnDR00OtHwcwe7df&#43;dvFz4fyNReFlfzDPwx2tzIWxJWljjw2UtIUUXY6iSV2TTx0=" target="_blank">
academic advisor</a>. If you have an SF Financial hold, you should pay your fall 2019 fee balance. Contact the
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fbronco-advising-center%252Findex.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138679203&amp;sdata=nXW%2BC%2BdOqmUWQYmSHzdH3hwcdXSDgjVKoMzTFDkrdKs%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fbronco-advising-center%2Findex.shtml" shash="btwh1&#43;DY&#43;varoq4wkvAcTuJywCoxklCJcQfVOEiCq&#43;aR9ZY2NF3ZgTZ4dl92G2A6RDb8UCJx5mnKmfwovWit4JjKwMP7pyKbysRKnNn5JhLkjzW8aWYJH4e1VbcHcwA7QXX7E6&#43;04E9Ri9VSl9ER7SdPvr3y8NYUpGbo/W5f9j8=" target="_blank">
Bronco Advising Center</a> if you have follow up questions about your balance.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo2">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">If you need a permission number, start by contacting the
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudentsuccess%252Fdirectories%252Fdepartments-az.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138679203&amp;sdata=5komb5%2FkHAQlq7uTafb8U%2BTWCiV1tc7hPks7snz3dj8%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudentsuccess%2Fdirectories%2Fdepartments-az.shtml" shash="vb6iR05XtFLAzMgL4mkxuQX5dTeqHycOp1WIKy5ozM/yOhgEZgYODY1c9VnQ6JszKZFloSmKtBDA0gHbiEsWmebC1CsJTlT9EsA7M1GavB5ytSgNCMbgj0l1WrB8UrHUI8jO2ohKRYc6rJPnelIfOv6Sla3LHskqisnIEWDVUIk=" target="_blank">
academic department</a> offering the course.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo3">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">You'll get a requisite error if you try to enroll in waitlisted lecture and lab corequisites. Both the lecture and lab have to be open for you to enroll.
<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo4">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">General Registration continues through December 4. You have this time to continue to make adjustments to your schedule. You will have another opportunity to change your schedule during Add/Drop Period, which begins
 January 6.<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo5">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">During General Registration, the unit limit is 16 units. During Add/Drop, the unit limit is 18 units. Waitlisted units are part of your unit limit.<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:black;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;,sans-serif">The fee payment deadline is December 5. If you are receiving financial aid, this deadline does not apply to you. Student Accounting &amp; Cashiering Services also offers a
<a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fr20.rs6.net%2Ftn.jsp%3Ft%3Dui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0%26id%3Dpreview%26r%3D3%26p%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.cpp.edu%252F%257Estudent-accounting%252Findex.shtml&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7C8aaefbee11e4467799c508d763dff788%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637087694138689203&amp;sdata=DIxciJfkehGGzK9TIfvrSeXxg8h8rXAF9Nh79pFqF9Q%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?t=ui6cyt4ab.0.0.iswwm5sab.0&amp;id=preview&amp;r=3&amp;p=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cpp.edu%2F%7Estudent-accounting%2Findex.shtml" shash="mlCjFqQGgIt1gSPgFTLB7c2j0qyfKHz&#43;joEknkQS3FjLkiOA40vMfSZwNB0M6cr0H/njDPoj2pvrNk74sp1sSQELONuse9P40twE3pfcoOoEoghtiVcgGCH6JUvhV5b8qQumDdBoI3jnJgJyWWp1GNgvzI3wPtSM&#43;MhEmwN5D7U=" target="_blank">
monthly payment plan</a> to all students. Financial aid disburses approximately 10 days before the first day of the term.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></li></ul>
<div>

<td valign="top" style="padding:0in 13.5pt 6.75pt 13.5pt">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;;color:#202020"><br>
</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#202020">Broncos,<br>
&nbsp;<br>
</span><em><b><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#002060;font-style:normal">Focus on Finals</span></b></em><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#002060">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#202020">returns for
 the final two weeks of Fall Semester - Dec. 2 - 15 with free food, extended study hours, and relaxation spaces &amp; events. (Yes,&nbsp;th</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#3B3838">is</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#202020">&nbsp;means
 therapy dogs!)<br>
&nbsp;<br>
</span><em><b><span style="font-size:15.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:navy">What is It?</span></b></em><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#202020"><br>
<br>
Focus on Finals&nbsp;is two weeks dedicated to&nbsp;<em><span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif">you</span></em>.&nbsp;Students can access free test supplies, extended study hours at the&nbsp;University&nbsp;Library, BSC, and BRIC, healthy snacks, free food &amp; drink events, and
 workshops/space dedicated to de-stress and recharge.<br>
&nbsp;<br>
</span><em><b><span style="font-size:15.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:navy">What Should I Look Out For?</span></b></em><span style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;;color:#202020">
<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#202020;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:150%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1;-ms-text-size-adjust: 100%;-webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%">
<span style="font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif">&quot;Finals Stations&quot;&nbsp;across campus will have&nbsp;free Scantrons, blue books, stress balls, and more. Just look for the blue banners and Focus on Finals logo on Monday to Thursday of finals week (Dec. 9-12).</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;"><o:p></o:p></span></li><li class="MsoNormal" style="color:#202020;mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:150%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1;-ms-text-size-adjust: 100%;-webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%">

<p class="MsoNormal">If your application was <span style="background:yellow;mso-highlight:yellow">

 you can get the contract from the department office then and have it signed by the instructor and returned to me.&nbsp;

 will be performing </span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;color:#201F1E"><br>
</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">maintenance to the campus wireless network on Saturday, December 21,

</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">2019 from 10:00 PM to 11:59 PM.</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;color:#201F1E"><br>
<br>
</span><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">What does this mean to me?:</span></b><span style="font-size:12.0pt;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">&nbsp; You may experience intermittent wireless
</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;color:#201F1E"><br>
</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">network outages throughout the campus for up to one hour starting at 10:00
</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;color:#201F1E"><br>
</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;border:none windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in">PM on Saturday, December 21, 2019 until 11:59 PM.</span><span style="font-size:12.0pt;color:#201F1E"><br>

<div class="WordSection1">
<p class="MsoNormal">Dear all,<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">As part of the <a href="https://nam03.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdot.ca.gov%2Fcaltrans-near-me%2Fdistrict-7%2Fdistrict-7-projects%2Fd7-i10-hov-san-bernardino&amp;data=02%7C01%7Ccjkeenan%40cpp.edu%7Cb0bab85ccee54fbfcd5808d795479a4c%7C164ba61e39ec4f5d89ffaa1f00a521b4%7C0%7C0%7C637142010349087658&amp;sdata=qT1rk%2FqZOGhq0Dnb4e3VganWtVwQuuBTHIYh5%2BHJsyM%3D&amp;reserved=0" originalsrc="https://dot.ca.gov/caltrans-near-me/district-7/district-7-projects/d7-i10-hov-san-bernardino" shash="j/2BDYg0qvYEDcN7Dv6&#43;y4V9957Xy4cClR&#43;NSsrrh6HWakspIFiYvCZtnnMB0Fae6mjPLn1HObZhjt5kBojAf7hrFS4Zp5o/1D4z0hkJy8nKOnMbzVYNmdPADmVkZ4gdxd1nlMFTUgaPRYGANEMDWQ/6UAJPTOarS32y6sfkF&#43;g=">
San Bernardino Freeway (I-10) High Occupancy Vehicle Lane Project</a>, Caltrans has informed us that the previously announced closure of the off-ramp to Kellogg Drive from eastbound I-10 will tentatively begin Jan. 15, 2020. The closure is expected to last
 for 90 days. We will provide updates to campus via email, social media, <a href="http://polycentric.cpp.edu/">
PolyCentric</a>, and the university’s <a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~compass/">Compass website</a> once Caltrans confirms the closure start date.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">We can expect that this closure will increase traffic at the Grand Avenue and Fairplex exits during the morning commute hours. Please plan accordingly to ensure safe and timely travel to campus. Alternate routes can be found at the university’s
<a href="https://www.cpp.edu/~compass/">Compass website</a>.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Thank you for your patience and cooperation.<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Chief D. Robinson<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">University Police Department<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<body style="word-wrap: break-word; -webkit-nbsp-mode: space; line-break: after-white-space;" class="">
I think the green petition you are referring to is for prereq waiver, all our graduate courses have graduate standing as prereq and you would need a waiver to get into them.&nbsp;
<div class=""><br class="">
</div>
<div class="">To get a graduate course to count towards your degree, you need to file a general academic petition. Please note if you do so, you will not be able to use this course as a graduate course if you decided to pursue a Masters at CPP (no double counting
 is allowed).</div>
<div class=""><br class="">
</div>
<div class="">Let me know if you have other questions<br class="">
<div><br class="">

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#C00000">This email is sent on behalf of Dr. Ron Yeung:</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Dear Engineering Faculty and Students,</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Each year, the university honors one outstanding faculty advisor from each college.&nbsp; Please note that nominations are now accepted for this year’s College of Engineering Outstanding Faculty Advisor Award.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Nominations shall include a statement to the Selection Committee addressing the following selection criteria.</span></b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Selection Criteria</span></b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Selection of the College Outstanding Faculty Advisor shall be based on criteria from the following list. It is not expected or required that faculty advisors meet all of these criteria.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">The nominee:</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">a) Communicates with advisees professionally, allowing an appropriate amount of time to discuss a variety of subjects related to advisees’ educational programs, including and recognizing their unique backgrounds
 and needs;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">b) Assists advisees in assessing their interests and abilities, examining their educational goals, and developing short-term and long-term plans to meet their objectives;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">c) Periodically reviews the academic progress of the advisees and its impact on achievement of goals and seek practical, thorough, innovative, and timely solutions to advisees’ problems;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">d) Makes advisees aware of, and refers them to, qualified persons and educational, institutional, and community resources, programs, and services;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">e) Understands, interprets, and accurately communicates policies, procedures, and information to assist advisees to make well-informed academic decisions; and</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">f) Seeks opportunities to grow professionally as an advisor and shares his or her advising philosophies and techniques with colleagues.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size:12.0pt">All nominations are due by 5:00 pm, March 4, 2020 to Mary Shoo, via email to
<a href="mailto:engineering@cpp.edu"><span style="color:windowtext;text-decoration:none">mmshoo</span></a>@cpp.edu.</span></b><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Please feel free to contact me if you have any questions.</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Sincerely,</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Ron</span><o:p></o:p></p>
